The `number of followers` of users in China on `2025/4/25 9:46 PM UTC`. This list contains users from `China` and cities `Beijing` `Shanghai` `Guangzhou` `Shenzhen` `Chongqing` `Chengdu` `Harbin` `Tianjin`.

There are `138 countries` and `674 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/gayanvoice/top-github-users).

There are `936 users`  in China. You need at least `764 followers` to be on this list.

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
